Do not overload this page with your ads: That's what your own pages are for. Blog posts may or may not be allowed, depending on the content and frequency. Personal blog posts will likely be removed. Real estate ads will be allowed to remain up only for a few days. Clothing ads will be allowed only for locally owned sellers of Indian clothing. Restaurant/catering ads will be allowed only for local Indian food. Event ads will be allowed for only Austin-area Indian-oriented events. Ad posts that feature a person may be posted only by that person. Biz ads with a picture of or person or a review by a person will be removed; we do not know if you have that person's permission to post their likeness. Any post may be removed at any time at the discretion of the admins.
